###These events assign the racial traits on birth and make stillborn children of unions that are not allowed########

namespace = racialbirth

character_event = {
	id = racialbirth.0
	hide_window = yes

#Now we kill all children of dis-allowed racial unions
character_event = {
	id = racialbirth.1
	# desc = EVTDESCCHAOS.10 #hidden, doesnt matter
	# picture = "GFX_evt_daemons" #hidden, doesnt matter
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes #on_birth
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = adopted }
		OR = {
			OR = {
				true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_illithid }
				mother_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_illithid }
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_human }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_half_orc }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_half_elf }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_half_dwarf }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_half_ogre }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_half_giant }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_gith }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_tiefling }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_genasi }
					true_father_even_if_dead = { trait = creature_aasimar }
				}
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_human } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_elf } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_sea_elf } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_drow } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_feyri } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_eladrin } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_orc } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_ogre } }		
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_half_elf } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_half_dwarf } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_half_orc } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_half_ogre } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_half_giant } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_ogrillon } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_pureblood } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_gith } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_giant } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_hobgoblin } }
				mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { trait = creature_bugbear } }
